{

               NLD=Hoofdprojectkosten per ksrt/periode];
    OnPreReport=BEGIN
                  IF (PeriodFilter = '') OR (CumulationFilter = '') THEN
                    ERROR(Text000);

                  DateSelectionManagement.ConvertPeriodStringToDates(PeriodFilter, DateFilterStart, DateFilterEnd);

                  MainProject.SETFILTER("Cumulation Filter", CumulationFilter);

                  DeterminePeriods;
                END;

    { 1100525004;;DataItem;MainProject       ;
               DataItemTable=Table11072003;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(No.)
                                 WHERE(Single/Main/Sub Project=CONST(Main Project));
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               DPA_SetFilters(CurrReport.OBJECTID(FALSE));
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  CreateCostControl.RUN(MainProject);

                                  SETRANGE("Period Filter", DateFilterStart, DateFilterEnd);
                                  SETRANGE("Cumulation Filter", 0D, DateFilterEnd);
                                  IF GETRANGEMIN("Period Filter") = GETRANGEMAX("Period Filter") THEN
                                    SETRANGE("Period Filter", GETRANGEMIN("Period Filter"));

                                  SearchProgrDate.DetermineDate(MainProject, FALSE);
                                  SearchPrognDate.DetermineDate(MainProject);

                                  IF Project.GET("No.") THEN BEGIN
                                    Project.DPA_SetFilters(CurrReport.OBJECTID(FALSE));
                                    Project.SETFILTER("Project Filter", "No.");
                                    Project.SETRANGE("Single/Main/Sub Project", "Single/Main/Sub Project"::"Sub Project");
                                    Project.SETRANGE("Cumulation Filter", 0D, PeriodStartDate[8]-1);

                                    Project.CALCFIELDS(Revenues);
                                    ProjectRevenuesBeforePeriods := Project.Revenues;
                                    ProjectRevenues := Project.Revenues;

                                    FOR i := 1 TO 8 DO BEGIN
                                      Project.SETRANGE("Period Filter", PeriodStartDate[i], PeriodEndDate[i]);
                                      Project.CALCFIELDS("Revenues Period");
                                      RevenuesPeriod[i] := Project."Revenues Period";
                                      ProjectRevenues += Project."Revenues Period";
                                    END;

                                    Project.SETRANGE("Period Filter", DateFilterStart, DateFilterEnd);
                                    Project.CALCFIELDS("Revenues Period");
                                    RevenuesEntirePeriod := Project."Revenues Period";
                                    ProjectRevenues += Project."Revenues Period";
                                  END;

                                  Project.SETRANGE("Main Project", "No.");
                                  IF Project.FINDSET THEN
                                    REPEAT
                                      Project.SETFILTER("Project Filter", Project."No.");
                                      Project.SETRANGE("Cumulation Filter", 0D, PeriodStartDate[8]-1);

                                      Project.CALCFIELDS(Revenues);
                                      ProjectRevenuesBeforePeriods += Project.Revenues;
                                      ProjectRevenues += Project.Revenues;

                                      FOR i := 1 TO 8 DO BEGIN
                                        Project.SETRANGE("Period Filter", PeriodStartDate[i], PeriodEndDate[i]);
                                        Project.CALCFIELDS("Revenues Period");
                                        RevenuesPeriod[i] += Project."Revenues Period";
                                        ProjectRevenues += Project."Revenues Period";
                                      END;

                                      Project.SETRANGE("Period Filter", DateFilterStart, DateFilterEnd);
                                      Project.CALCFIELDS("Revenues Period");
                                      RevenuesEntirePeriod += Project."Revenues Period";
                                      ProjectRevenues += Project."Revenues Period";
                                    UNTIL Project.NEXT = 0;

                                  ProjectRevenuesBeforePeriodsTotal += ProjectRevenuesBeforePeriods;
                                  RevenuesPeriodTotal[8] += RevenuesPeriod[8];
                                  RevenuesPeriodTotal[7] += RevenuesPeriod[7];
                                  RevenuesPeriodTotal[6] += RevenuesPeriod[6];
                                  RevenuesPeriodTotal[5] += RevenuesPeriod[5];
                                  RevenuesPeriodTotal[4] += RevenuesPeriod[4];
                                  RevenuesPeriodTotal[3] += RevenuesPeriod[3];
                                  RevenuesPeriodTotal[2] += RevenuesPeriod[2];
                                  RevenuesPeriodTotal[1] += RevenuesPeriod[1];
                                  RevenuesEntirePeriodTotal += RevenuesEntirePeriod;
                                  ProjectRevenuesTotal += ProjectRevenues;
                                END;

               ReqFilterFields=No. }

    { 1100525007;1;DataItem;MainProjectCostType;
               DataItemTable=Table11012046;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Project No.,Cost Type);
               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  SETFILTER("Project Filter", '');
                                  SETRANGE("Cumulation Filter", 0D, PeriodStartDate[8]-1);
                                  CALCFIELDS("Actual Costs");
                                  ActualCostsBeforePeriods := "Actual Costs";
                                  ActualCosts := "Actual Costs";

                                  CASE "Cost Type" OF
                                    "Cost Type"::Labor: ActualCostsBeforePeriodsLaborTotal += "Actual Costs";
                                    "Cost Type"::Material: ActualCostsBeforePeriodsMaterialTotal += "Actual Costs";
                                    "Cost Type"::Subcontracting: ActualCostsBeforePeriodsSubcontractingTotal += "Actual Costs";
                                    "Cost Type"::Plant: ActualCostsBeforePeriodsPlantTotal += "Actual Costs";
                                    "Cost Type"::Sundry: ActualCostsBeforePeriodsSundryTotal += "Actual Costs";
                                  END;

                                  FOR i := 1 TO 8 DO BEGIN
                                    SETRANGE("Period Filter", PeriodStartDate[i], PeriodEndDate[i]);
                                    CALCFIELDS("Actuals Period");
                                    ActualsPeriod[i] := "Actuals Period";
                                    ActualCosts := ActualCosts + "Actuals Period";

                                    CASE "Cost Type" OF
                                      "Cost Type"::Labor: ActualsPeriodLaborTotal[i] += "Actuals Period";
                                      "Cost Type"::Material: ActualsPeriodMaterialTotal[i] += "Actuals Period";
                                      "Cost Type"::Subcontracting: ActualsPeriodSubcontractingTotal[i] += "Actuals Period";
                                      "Cost Type"::Plant: ActualsPeriodPlantTotal[i] += "Actuals Period";
                                      "Cost Type"::Sundry: ActualsPeriodSundryTotal[i] += "Actuals Period";
                                    END;
                                  END;

                                  SETRANGE("Period Filter", DateFilterStart, DateFilterEnd);
                                  CALCFIELDS("Actuals Period");

                                  ActualsEntirePeriod := "Actuals Period";
                                  ActualCosts := ActualCosts + "Actuals Period";

                                  CASE "Cost Type" OF
                                    "Cost Type"::Labor:
                                      BEGIN
                                        ActualsEntirePeriodLaborTotal += "Actuals Period";
                                        ActualsLaborTotal += ActualCosts;
                                      END;
                                    "Cost Type"::Material:
                                      BEGIN
                                        ActualsEntirePeriodMaterialTotal += "Actuals Period";
                                        ActualsMaterialTotal += ActualCosts;
                                      END;
                                    "Cost Type"::Subcontracting:
                                      BEGIN
                                        ActualsEntirePeriodSubcontractingTotal += "Actuals Period";
                                        ActualsSubcontractingTotal += ActualCosts;
                                      END;
                                    "Cost Type"::Plant:
                                      BEGIN
                                        ActualsEntirePeriodPlantTotal += "Actuals Period";
                                        ActualsPlantTotal += ActualCosts;
                                      END;
                                    "Cost Type"::Sundry:
                                      BEGIN
                                        ActualsEntirePeriodSundryTotal += "Actuals Period";
                                        ActualsSundryTotal += ActualCosts;
                                      END;
                                  END;

                                  ActualCostsBeforePeriodsTotal += ActualCostsBeforePeriods;
                                  ActualsPeriodTotal[8] += ActualsPeriod[8];
                                  ActualsPeriodTotal[7] += ActualsPeriod[7];
                                  ActualsPeriodTotal[6] += ActualsPeriod[6];
                                  ActualsPeriodTotal[5] += ActualsPeriod[5];
                                  ActualsPeriodTotal[4] += ActualsPeriod[4];
                                  ActualsPeriodTotal[3] += ActualsPeriod[3];
                                  ActualsPeriodTotal[2] += ActualsPeriod[2];
                                  ActualsPeriodTotal[1] += ActualsPeriod[1];
                                  ActualsEntirePeriodTotal += ActualsEntirePeriod;
                                  ActualCostsTotal += ActualCosts;
                                END;

               DataItemLink=Project No.=FIELD(No.) }

    PROCEDURE GetReportName@1100525003() : Text;
    BEGIN
      EXIT(DELSTR(CurrReport.OBJECTID, 1, STRPOS(CurrReport.OBJECTID, ' ')));
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetReportFilter@1100525000() : Text;
    VAR
      ProjectFilter0@1100525000 : Text;
      ProjectFilter2@1100525001 : Text;
    BEGIN
      ProjectFilter0 := MainProject.GETFILTERS;
      MainProject.FILTERGROUP(2);
      ProjectFilter2 := MainProject.GETFILTERS;
      MainProject.FILTERGROUP(0);

      IF (ProjectFilter0 = '') AND (ProjectFilter2 = '') THEN
        EXIT;

      IF ProjectFilter2 <> '' THEN
        EXIT(STRSUBSTNO('%1: %2, %3', MainProject.TABLECAPTION, ProjectFilter0, ProjectFilter2))
      ELSE
        EXIT(STRSUBSTNO('%1: %2', MainProject.TABLECAPTION, ProjectFilter0));
    END;

    PROCEDURE DeterminePeriods@1100409001();
    VAR
      I@1100525002 : Integer;
      CumulationFilter@1100525005 : Text;
    BEGIN
      FOR I := 1 TO 8 DO
        PeriodManagementReports.FindPeriod(PeriodStartDate[I], PeriodEndDate[I], CumulationFilter, PeriodFilter, PeriodType, '<=');
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetPeriodSelection@1100409000(PeriodType@1100409000 : 'Day,Week,Month,Quarter,Year,AccountingPeriod') PeriodTypeText : Text;
    VAR
      Text001@1100409006 : TextConst 'DEU=Tag;ENU=Day;NLD=Dag;NOR=Dag;SVE=Dag';
      Text002@1100409005 : TextConst 'DEU=Woche;ENU=Week;NLD=Week;NOR=Uke;SVE=Vecka';
      Text003@1100409004 : TextConst 'DEU=Monat;ENU=Month;NLD=Maand;NOR=MÜned;SVE=MÜnad';
      Text004@1100409003 : TextConst 'DEU=Quartal;ENU=Quarter;NLD=Kwartaal;NOR=Kvartal;SVE=Kvartal';
      Text005@1100409002 : TextConst 'DEU=Jahr;ENU=Year;NLD=Jaar;NOR=èr;SVE=èr';
      Text006@1100409001 : TextConst 'DEU=Buchhaltungsperiode;ENU=Accounting Period;NLD=Boekhoudperiode;NOR=Regnskapsperiode;SVE=Bokfîringsperiod';
    BEGIN
      CASE PeriodType OF
        PeriodType::Day : PeriodTypeText:= Text001;
        PeriodType::Week : PeriodTypeText:= Text002;
        PeriodType::Month : PeriodTypeText:= Text003;
        PeriodType::Quarter : PeriodTypeText:= Text004;
        PeriodType::Year : PeriodTypeText:= Text005;
        PeriodType::AccountingPeriod : PeriodTypeText:= Text006;
      END;
    END;

    BEGIN
    END.

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function
